</table>
<p>The <b><a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="FIFA U-17 World Cup">FIFA U-16 World Championship</a> 1987</b>, the second edition of the tournament, was hosted by <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> and held in the cities of <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_John,_New_Brunswick" title="Saint John, New Brunswick">Saint John</a>, <a href="/wiki/St._John%27s,_Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="St. John's, Newfoundland and Labrador">St. John's</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a> between 12 July and 25 July 1987. Players born after 1 August 1970 could participate in this tournament.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Venues">Venues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1987_FIFA_U-16_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Venues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The cities of <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_John,_New_Brunswick" title="Saint John, New Brunswick">Saint John</a>, <a href="/wiki/St._John%27s,_Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="St. John's, Newfoundland and Labrador">St. John's</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a> hosted tournament matches.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Goalscorers">Goalscorers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1987_FIFA_U-16_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Goalscorers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Moussa Traoré of Ivory Coast won the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Cup#Awards" title="FIFA U-17 World Cup">Golden Shoe</a> award for scoring five goals. In total, 82 goals were scored by 54 different players, with none of them credited as own goal.</p>
<dl>
<dt>5 goals</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast"><img alt="Ivory Coast" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire.svg/23px-Flag_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire.svg/35px-Flag_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire.svg/45px-Flag_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Traor%C3%A9_(footballer,_born_1971)" title="Moussa Traoré (footballer, born 1971)">Moussa Traoré</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union"><img alt="Soviet Union" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1200" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_the_Soviet_Union.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Soviet_Union.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_the_Soviet_Union.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Soviet_Union.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Flag_of_the_Soviet_Union.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Soviet_Union.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yuri_Nikiforov" title="Yuri Nikiforov">Yuri Nikiforov</a></li>
</ul>

<td>16</td>
<td style="text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="1000" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/23px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/35px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/46px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Canada_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="Canada men's national soccer team">Canada</a></span></td>

<p>FIFA awarded the Golden Boot to <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Traor%C3%A9_(footballer,_born_1971)" title="Moussa Traoré (footballer, born 1971)">Moussa Traoré</a> because Côte d'Ivoire had scored fewer goals than USSR.</p>
